Interface TypeScript - Retirada AutomÃ¡tica

interface ConnectionWithdrawalConfig {
  enabled: boolean;
  daysBeforeWithdraw: number;        // 7-30
  actionAfterWithdraw:
    | 'nothing'
    | 'add_to_list'                  // Lista "NÃ£o conectou"
    | 'retry_in_30_days'
    | 'permanent_blacklist';
  notifyOnWithdraw: boolean;
  minPendingThreshold: number;        // SÃ³ retira se pendentes > X
}

interface PendingConnection {
  id: string;
  linkedinAccountId: string;
  targetProfileUrl: string;
  targetName: string;
  targetHeadline: string;
  sentAt: Date;
  campaignId?: string;
  status: 'pending' | 'accepted' | 'withdrawn' | 'declined';
  withdrawnAt?: Date;
  withdrawReason?: 'auto' | 'manual' | 'limit_reached';
}

// Job de retirada (executa diariamente Ã s 03:00)
async function processAutomaticWithdrawals(accountId: string): Promise<WithdrawalResult> {
  const config = await getWithdrawalConfig(accountId);
  if (!config.enabled) return { withdrawn: 0 };

  const pendingCount = await countPendingConnections(accountId);
  if (pendingCount < config.minPendingThreshold) return { withdrawn: 0 };

  const cutoffDate = subDays(new Date(), config.daysBeforeWithdraw);
  const eligibleConnections = await getPendingConnectionsBefore(accountId, cutoffDate);

  const results: WithdrawalResult = { withdrawn: 0, failed: 0, errors: [] };

  for (const connection of eligibleConnections) {
    try {
      await withdrawConnection(accountId, connection.targetProfileUrl);
      await updateConnectionStatus(connection.id, 'withdrawn', 'auto');

      // AÃ§Ã£o pÃ³s-retirada
      switch (config.actionAfterWithdraw) {
        case 'add_to_list':
          await addToList(accountId, 'nao_conectou', connection.targetProfileUrl);
          break;
        case 'retry_in_30_days':
          await scheduleRetry(connection, 30);
          break;
        case 'permanent_blacklist':
          await addToBlacklist(accountId, connection.targetProfileUrl);
          break;
      }

      results.withdrawn++;
      await randomDelay(3000, 8000); // Rate limiting
    } catch (error) {
      results.failed++;
      results.errors.push({ connectionId: connection.id, error: error.message });
    }
  }

  if (config.notifyOnWithdraw && results.withdrawn > 0) {
    await sendNotification(accountId, `${results.withdrawn} convites retirados automaticamente`);
  }

  return results;
}

Sistema de Lead Scoring

Fatores de PontuaÃ§Ã£o (0-100)

Fator Peso Como Calcula Exemplos
Engajamento 25 pts Quantidade e qualidade das interaÃ§Ãµes +5 por msg enviada, +10 por resposta, +15 por pergunta sobre preÃ§o
Profile Fit 25 pts Match com ICP (Ideal Customer Profile) Cargo C-level +15, Empresa 50+ func +10, Setor alvo +10
Velocidade 25 pts Tempo de resposta do lead Resposta em <1h +25, <4h +15, <24h +10, >24h +5
Sinais de IntenÃ§Ã£o 25 pts Palavras/aÃ§Ãµes que indicam interesse "preÃ§o" +10, "demo" +15, "quando podemos" +20, "contrato" +25

ClassificaÃ§Ã£o por Temperatura

Temperatura Score AÃ§Ã£o Recomendada SLA
ğŸ”¥ HOT 80-100 Prioridade mÃ¡xima, ligar/agendar AGORA Contato em 1h
ğŸŸ¡ WARM 50-79 Nutrir com conteÃºdo, follow-up Contato em 24h
â„ï¸ COLD 0-49 SequÃªncia de nurturing automÃ¡tica AutomaÃ§Ã£o

Algoritmo de Scoring

interface ScoreCalculation {
  engagement: {
    messagesReceived: number;      // +5 cada (max 15)
    questionsAsked: number;        // +8 cada (max 16)
    priceInquiry: boolean;         // +10
    demoRequest: boolean;          // +15
    meetingScheduled: boolean;     // +25
  };

  profileFit: {
    jobTitleMatch: 'exact' | 'partial' | 'none';  // +15/+8/+0
    companySizeMatch: boolean;                     // +10
    industryMatch: boolean;                        // +10
    locationMatch: boolean;                        // +5
  };

  responseTime: {
    avgResponseMinutes: number;
    // <60min = 25pts, <240min = 15pts, <1440min = 10pts, else 5pts
  };

  intentSignals: {
    mentionedBudget: boolean;      // +10
    mentionedTimeline: boolean;    // +10
    mentionedPain: boolean;        // +8
    askedHowItWorks: boolean;      // +5
    requestedProposal: boolean;    // +20
  };
}

function calculateLeadScore(lead: Lead, interactions: Interaction[]): number {
  let score = 0;

  // Engagement (max 25)
  const msgCount = interactions.filter(i => i.direction === 'inbound').length;
  score += Math.min(msgCount * 5, 15);

  const hasPrice = interactions.some(i =>
    i.content.toLowerCase().match(/pre[Ã§c]o|valor|quanto custa|investimento/)
  );
  if (hasPrice) score += 10;

  // Profile Fit (max 25)
  if (isDecisionMaker(lead.jobTitle)) score += 15;
  if (lead.companySize >= 50) score += 10;

  // Response Time (max 25)
  const avgResponse = calculateAvgResponseTime(interactions);
  if (avgResponse < 60) score += 25;
  else if (avgResponse < 240) score += 15;
  else if (avgResponse < 1440) score += 10;
  else score += 5;

  // Intent Signals (max 25)
  const hasDemo = interactions.some(i =>
    i.content.toLowerCase().match(/demo|demonstra[Ã§c][aÃ£]o|apresenta[Ã§c][aÃ£]o|reuniÃ£o/)
  );
  if (hasDemo) score += 15;

  return Math.min(score, 100);
}

Schema de Banco de Dados (Adicional)

-- Convites Pendentes (para retirada automÃ¡tica)
CREATE TABLE pending_connections (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  target_profile_url VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
  target_name VARCHAR(200),
  target_headline VARCHAR(500),
  campaign_id UUID REFERENCES campaigns(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  sent_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
  status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending', -- pending, accepted, withdrawn, declined
  withdrawn_at TIMESTAMP,
  withdraw_reason VARCHAR(20), -- auto, manual, limit_reached
  retry_scheduled_at TIMESTAMP,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),

  UNIQUE(linkedin_account_id, target_profile_url)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_pending_connections_status ON pending_connections(linkedin_account_id, status, sent_at);

-- ConfiguraÃ§Ã£o de Retirada por Conta
CREATE TABLE withdrawal_configs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE UNIQUE,
  enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  days_before_withdraw INTEGER DEFAULT 14 CHECK (days_before_withdraw BETWEEN 7 AND 30),
  action_after_withdraw VARCHAR(30) DEFAULT 'nothing', -- nothing, add_to_list, retry_in_30_days, permanent_blacklist
  notify_on_withdraw BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  min_pending_threshold INTEGER DEFAULT 500,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- HistÃ³rico de Retiradas
CREATE TABLE withdrawal_history (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  execution_date DATE NOT NULL,
  total_pending INTEGER,
  eligible_count INTEGER,
  withdrawn_count INTEGER,
  failed_count INTEGER,
  errors JSONB,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

  is_won_stage BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  is_lost_stage BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),

  UNIQUE(project_id, code),
  UNIQUE(project_id, position)
);

-- TABELAS CRÃTICAS DE SEGURANÃ‡A E OPERAÃ‡ÃƒO

-- Gerenciamento de Chaves de Criptografia
CREATE TABLE encryption_keys (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  key_name VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,           -- 'linkedin_sessions', 'api_tokens', etc.
  key_version INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
  encrypted_key BYTEA NOT NULL,                     -- Chave criptografada com master key (AWS KMS/Vault)
  algorithm VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'AES-256-GCM',
  status VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'active',              -- active, rotating, deprecated, revoked
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  rotated_at TIMESTAMP,
  expires_at TIMESTAMP,
  created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id)
);

-- HistÃ³rico de RotaÃ§Ã£o de Chaves (Auditoria)
CREATE TABLE key_rotation_log (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  key_id UUID REFERENCES encryption_keys(id),
  old_version INTEGER,
  new_version INTEGER,
  reason VARCHAR(200),                              -- scheduled, compromised, policy
  rotated_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  rotated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Rate Limiting por Conta LinkedIn
CREATE TABLE rate_limits (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  action_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,                 -- connection_request, message, profile_view, etc.
  window_start TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
  window_duration_minutes INTEGER DEFAULT 60,
  count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  limit_value INTEGER NOT NULL,                     -- Limite mÃ¡ximo para esta janela
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  UNIQUE(linkedin_account_id, action_type, window_start)
);

-- Limites DiÃ¡rios Consolidados
CREATE TABLE daily_limits (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  date DATE NOT NULL,
  action_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  used INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  limit_value INTEGER NOT NULL,
  limit_reduced BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,              -- Se limite foi reduzido por warning
  reduction_reason VARCHAR(200),
  UNIQUE(linkedin_account_id, date, action_type)
);

-- Logs de Erro Detalhados
CREATE TABLE error_logs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id),
  campaign_id UUID,
  lead_id UUID,

  error_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,                 -- linkedin_rate_limit, captcha_required, etc.
  error_code VARCHAR(50),
  error_message TEXT,
  stack_trace TEXT,

  context JSONB,                                    -- Dados adicionais do erro
  request_data JSONB,                               -- Dados da requisiÃ§Ã£o que causou erro

  severity VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'error',             -- debug, info, warning, error, critical
  is_recoverable BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,

  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  resolved_at TIMESTAMP,
  resolved_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  resolution_notes TEXT
);

-- Circuit Breaker State
CREATE TABLE circuit_breaker_state (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE UNIQUE,
  state VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'closed',               -- closed, open, half_open
  failure_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  success_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
  last_failure_at TIMESTAMP,
  last_success_at TIMESTAMP,
  opened_at TIMESTAMP,                              -- Quando abriu
  half_open_at TIMESTAMP,                           -- Quando entrou em half_open
  scheduled_close_at TIMESTAMP,                     -- Quando deve tentar fechar
  open_reason VARCHAR(200),                         -- rate_limit, captcha, restriction, etc.
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- HistÃ³rico do Circuit Breaker (para anÃ¡lise)
CREATE TABLE circuit_breaker_history (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  old_state VARCHAR(20),
  new_state VARCHAR(20),
  trigger_reason VARCHAR(200),
  failure_count_at_change INTEGER,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Alertas de SeguranÃ§a LinkedIn
CREATE TABLE linkedin_security_alerts (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  alert_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,                 -- captcha, restriction, warning, logout
  severity VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,                    -- low, medium, high, critical
  message TEXT,
  raw_response TEXT,                                -- Resposta original do LinkedIn
  action_taken VARCHAR(200),                        -- paused_account, reduced_limits, etc.
  acknowledged BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
  acknowledged_at TIMESTAMP,
  acknowledged_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Fingerprint do Browser por Conta
CREATE TABLE browser_fingerprints (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  linkedin_account_id UUID REFERENCES linkedin_accounts(id) ON DELETE CASCADE UNIQUE,
  user_agent TEXT NOT NULL,
  screen_resolution VARCHAR(20),
  color_depth INTEGER,
  timezone VARCHAR(100),
  language VARCHAR(20),
  platform VARCHAR(50),
  canvas_hash VARCHAR(64),
  webgl_vendor VARCHAR(200),
  webgl_renderer VARCHAR(200),
  plugins JSONB,
  fonts JSONB,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Ãndices para performance
CREATE INDEX idx_rate_limits_account_action ON rate_limits(linkedin_account_id, action_type, window_start DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_daily_limits_account_date ON daily_limits(linkedin_account_id, date DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_error_logs_account ON error_logs(linkedin_account_id, created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_error_logs_type ON error_logs(error_type, severity, created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_circuit_breaker_state ON circuit_breaker_state(linkedin_account_id, state);
CREATE INDEX idx_security_alerts_account ON linkedin_security_alerts(linkedin_account_id, created_at DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_security_alerts_unack ON linkedin_security_alerts(acknowledged, severity) WHERE acknowledged = FALSE;
